      * E10350 JJH 05/17/17 - Record selection with 6 Source Codes
      * Rtv Hog Pop Dist-Prd  Rt - Hog Population Dist  * 
     C                     EXSR SURVGN
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
      * Read the Carcass detail file
      * CASE: tattoo processing
      *  - c1 OR c2
      *   |- c1    : PAR.HRH Tattoo Number GT WRK.Zero USR
      *   |- c2    : PAR.Report Type Usr is Tattoo
      *   '-
     C           P2R6NB    IFGT WUE9NB                     *IF
     C           P1K9ST    OREQ 'T'                        *OR
      * no producer selected or no tattoo selected
      * CASE: producer blank, or tattoo number is zero
      *  - c1 AND c2
      *   |- c1    : PAR.PD Producer Code is Blank
      *   |- c2    : PAR.HRH Tattoo Number is Zero
      *   '-
     C                     MOVEL'0'       Y0CX01  1
     C           P4ABCD    IFEQ *BLANK                     *IF
     C           P2R6NB    IFEQ *ZERO                      *IF
     C                     MOVEL'1'       Y0CX01
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C           Y0CX01    IFEQ '1'                        *IF
      * Restrict by Co/ and Position on date
      * Rtv Hog Pop Crcs-Dte  Rt - Carcass Detail  * 
     C                     EXSR TORVGN
     C                     END                             *FI
      * Producer selection
      * CASE: PAR.PD Producer Code GT WRK.Blank USR
     C           P4ABCD    IFGT WUCRTX                     *IF
      * Restrict by Co/Producer and Position on date
      * Rtv Hog Pop Crcs-Prd  Rt - Carcass Detail  * 
     C                     EXSR NLRVGN
     C                     END                             *FI
      * Tattoo selection
      * CASE: PAR.HRH Tattoo Number GT WRK.Zero USR
     C           P2R6NB    IFGT WUE9NB                     *IF
      * Restrict by Co/tattoo number

     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: PAR.Report Type Usr is Company
     C           P1K9ST    IFEQ 'C'                        *IF
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    WUJBTX           HRD Report Brea
     C                     MOVELWUC3CD    WUJBTX           HRD Report Brea
      * Pass the nothing from the detail
      * Rtv Hog Pop f/build   RT - Hog Population Rpt Hdr  * 
     C                     EXSR THRVGN
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: PAR.Report Type Usr is Shift

     C                     Z-ADD1         ZQ      50
     C           WUC3CD    CAT  WGTMST:ZQ WUJBTX    P      HRD Report Brea
      * Pass the individual source code from the detail
      * Rtv Hog Pop f/build   RT - Hog Population Rpt Hdr  * 
     C                     EXSR TJRVGN
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
      * Check for report break
      * CASE: WRK.HRD Report Break NE WRK.Report Break Save

      * Rtv Hog Pop Dtl exists RT - Hog Population Rpt Dtl  * 
     C                     EXSR TLRVGN

     C                     PARM P5C9CD    WQ0041  6        Cutout Matrix C
     C                     PARM P5KLNB    WQ0042  40       Effective Month
      *
     C           *IN90     IFEQ '1'
      * Call to program ended in error
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0032' W0RTN
     C                     MOVEL*BLANKS   W0CLPG 10
     C                     MOVEL'PDT7XFR' W0CLPG
      * Send message '*Error occured on CALL...'
     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0032' ZAMSID

     C                     MOVELW0CLPG    ZAMSDA           Message data

     C                     SETON                     99    *
     C                     END
     C                     END                             *FI

      * RTV Hog Pop Tattoo Hdr XF - Tattoo Header  * 
     C                     CALL 'PKU5XFR'              90  RTV Hog Pop Tat
     C                     PARM *BLANK    W0RTN   7
     C                     PARM P2K1ST    WQ0043  1        HRH Type Of Dis
     C                     PARM WUJBTX    WQ0044 25        HRH Report Brea

      * Error detected?
     C           W0RTN     IFNE *BLANK

      * - Replace I Parm SR Source Code with TH Source Code-X18 USR
      * - Rtv Hog Pop Dist-Dte  Rt - Hog Population Dist

      *   - Substring TH Source Code-X18 USR into 6 Source Codes
      *   - Record Selection processing using 6 Source Codes
      * - Rtv Hog Pop Dist-Prd  Rt - Hog Population Dist
      *   - This function commented out, because of use with PKW6XFR
      *     which will not be modified at this time.

      *   - Record Selection processing using 6 Source Codes
      *   - Set the LCL.Source Code = Blank if TH Source Code-X18 = Blank
      *     LCL.SR Source Code = HPD Source Code from Hog Population Dist
      * - Rtv Hog Pop Crcs-Dte  Rt - Carcass Detail
      *   - Substring TH Source Code-X18 USR into 6 Source Codes
      *   - Record Selection processing using 6 Source Codes
      *   - Set the LCL.Source Code = Blank if TH Source Code-X18 = Blank
